2054	    @abstractmethod
2055	    def cmd_change_user(
2056	        self,
2057	        username: str = "",
2058	        password: str = "",
2059	        database: str = "",
2060	        charset: Optional[int] = None,
2061	        password1: str = "",
2062	        password2: str = "",
2063	        password3: str = "",
2064	        oci_config_file: str = "",
2065	        oci_config_profile: str = "",
2066	        openid_token_file: str = "",
2067	    ) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
2068	        """Changes the current logged in user.
2069	
2070	        It also causes the specified database to become the default (current)
2071	        database. It is also possible to change the character set using the
2072	        charset argument. The character set passed during initial connection
2073	        is reused if no value of charset is passed via this method.
2074	
2075	        Args:
2076	            username: New account's username.
2077	            password: New account's password.
2078	            database: Database to become the default (current) database.
2079	            charset: Client charset (see [1]), only the lower 8-bits.
2080	            password1: New account's password factor 1 - it's used instead
2081	                       of `password` if set (higher precedence).
2082	            password2: New account's password factor 2.
2083	            password3: New account's password factor 3.
2084	            oci_config_file: OCI configuration file location (path-like string).
2085	            oci_config_profile: OCI configuration profile location (path-like string).
2086	            openid_token_file: OpenID Connect token file location (path-like string).
2087	
2088	        Returns:
2089	            ok_packet: Dictionary containing the OK packet information.
2090	
2091	        Examples:
2092	            ```
2093	            >>> cnx.cmd_change_user(username='', password='', database='', charset=33)
2094	            ```
2095	
2096	        References:
2097	            [1]: https://dev.mysql.com/doc/dev/mysql-server/latest/\
2098	                page_protocol_basic_character_set.html#a_protocol_character_set

1052	        """Change the current logged in user
1053	
1054	        This method allows to change the current logged in user information.
1055	        The result is a dictionary with OK packet information.
1056	
1057	        Returns a dict()
1058	        """
1059	        # If charset isn't defined, we use the same charset ID defined previously,
1060	        # otherwise, we run a verification and update the charset ID.
1061	        if charset is not None:
1062	            if not isinstance(charset, int):
1063	                raise ValueError("charset must be an integer")
1064	            if charset < 0:
1065	                raise ValueError("charset should be either zero or a postive integer")
1066	            self._charset_id = charset
1067	
1068	        self._mfa_nfactor = 1
1069	        self._user = username
1070	        self._password = password
1071	        self._password1 = password1
1072	        self._password2 = password2
1073	        self._password3 = password3
1074	
1075	        if self._password1 and password != self._password1:
1076	            self._password = self._password1
1077	
1078	        self.handle_unread_result()
1079	
1080	        if self._compress:
1081	            raise NotSupportedError("Change user is not supported with compression")
1082	
1083	        if oci_config_file:
1084	            self._oci_config_file = oci_config_file
1085	        if openid_token_file:
1086	            self._openid_token_file = openid_token_file
1087	        self._oci_config_profile = oci_config_profile
1088	
1089	        # Update the custom configurations needed by specific auth plugins
1090	        self._authenticator.update_plugin_config(
1091	            config={
1092	                "oci_config_file": self._oci_config_file,
1093	                "oci_config_profile": self._oci_config_profile,
1094	                "openid_token_file": self._openid_token_file,
1095	            }
1096	        )
1097	
1098	        ok_pkt = self._authenticator.authenticate(
1099	            sock=self._socket,
1100	            handshake=self._handshake,
1101	            username=self._user,
1102	            password1=self._password,
1103	            password2=self._password2,
1104	            password3=self._password3,
1105	            database=database,
1106	            charset=self._charset_id,
1107	            client_flags=self._client_flags,
1108	            auth_plugin=self._auth_plugin,
1109	            auth_plugin_class=self._auth_plugin_class,
1110	            conn_attrs=self._conn_attrs,
1111	            is_change_user_request=True,
1112	        )
1113	
1114	        if not (self._client_flags & ClientFlag.CONNECT_WITH_DB) and database:
1115	            self.cmd_init_db(database)
1116
